    assert processing_loaded.get("status") == TaskStatus.PROCESSING.value


def test_internal_pipeline_executes_stage1_to_stage8(monkeypatch, tmp_path) -> None:  # type: ignore[no-untyped-def]
    monkeypatch.setenv("CLONECUT_DB_PATH", str(tmp_path / "clonecut_internal.db"))
    cfg = _build_config(tmp_path)
    cfg.raw["worker"]["use_internal_pipeline"] = True
    service = WorkerService(cfg)

    source = tmp_path / "internal-source.mp4"
    source.write_bytes(b"video-content" * 128)
    task = UnifiedTask(
        task_id="internal-pipeline-1",
        task_type=TaskType.VIDEO,
        source="unit",
        source_path=str(source),
        metadata={
            "source": "unit",
            "forum_post_info": {"thread_id": "123", "title": "topic"},
        },
    )

    captured: dict[str, object] = {}
    expected_output = Path(cfg.output_dir) / task.task_id / "final.mp4"

    class FakeVideoPipeline:
        def __init__(self, config, logger=None, performance_tracker=None, resource_monitor=None) -> None:  # type: ignore[no-untyped-def]
            captured["config_output_dir"] = config.output_dir
            captured["logger"] = logger
            captured["performance_tracker"] = performance_tracker
            captured["resource_monitor"] = resource_monitor

        def run(self, input_video, task_id, start_from_stage=0, forum_post_info=None):  # type: ignore[no-untyped-def]
            expected_output.parent.mkdir(parents=True, exist_ok=True)
            expected_output.write_bytes(b"final-video")
            captured["input_video"] = input_video
            captured["task_id"] = task_id
            captured["start_from_stage"] = start_from_stage
            captured["forum_post_info"] = forum_post_info
            return SimpleNamespace(
                success=True,
                output_file=str(expected_output),
                executed_stages=["stage1_transcode", "stage8_cover", "stage9_organize"],
                performance_summary="video pipeline ok",
                current_stage=11,
                last_stage="stage9_organize",
                failed_stage=None,
                performance_report=None,
            )

    monkeypatch.setattr("apps.worker.service.VideoPipeline", FakeVideoPipeline, raising=False)
    monkeypatch.setattr(
        "apps.worker.service.subprocess.run",
        lambda *args, **kwargs: (_ for _ in ()).throw(AssertionError("legacy subprocess path should not run")),
    )
    monkeypatch.setattr(
        service,
        "_run_internal_video_pipeline_fallback_copy",
        lambda *args, **kwargs: (_ for _ in ()).throw(AssertionError("fallback copy should not run")),
    )

    result = service._run_internal_video_pipeline(task, str(source))

    assert result.get("output_path") == str(expected_output)
    assert result.get("executed_mode") == "video_pipeline"
    executed = result.get("executed_stages") or []
    assert "stage1_transcode" in executed
    assert "stage8_cover" in executed
    assert captured["config_output_dir"] == str(Path(cfg.output_dir))
    assert captured["input_video"] == str(source)
    assert captured["task_id"] == task.task_id
    assert captured["start_from_stage"] == 0
    assert captured["forum_post_info"] == {"thread_id": "123", "title": "topic"}
    assert task.current_stage == 11
    assert task.stage_checkpoint == "stage9_organize"
    assert (Path(cfg.output_dir) / task.task_id / "forum_post_info.json").exists()
    state_payload = json.loads((Path(cfg.output_dir) / task.task_id / "state.json").read_text(encoding="utf-8"))
    assert state_payload["last_completed_step"] == 9
    assert state_payload["last_completed_step_name"] == "stage9_organize"
    assert state_payload["output_file"] == str(expected_output)


def test_attach_video_render_manifest_collects_primary_subtitle_cover_and_state(monkeypatch, tmp_path) -> None:  # type: ignore[no-untyped-def]
    monkeypatch.setenv("CLONECUT_DB_PATH", str(tmp_path / "clonecut_render_manifest.db"))
    cfg = _build_config(tmp_path)
    service = WorkerService(cfg)

    task_dir = Path(cfg.output_dir) / "render-manifest-task"
    task_dir.mkdir(parents=True, exist_ok=True)

    final_video = task_dir / "璁哄潧鏍锋湰_final.mp4"
    final_video.write_bytes(b"final-video")
    no_subtitle_video = task_dir / "璁哄潧鏍锋湰_鏅鸿兘鍓緫鏃犲瓧骞曠増.mp4"
    no_subtitle_video.write_bytes(b"no-subtitle")
    subtitle_srt = task_dir / "total.srt"
    subtitle_srt.write_text("1\n00:00:00,000 --> 00:00:01,000\nhello\n", encoding="utf-8")
    subtitle_ass = task_dir / "total.ass"
    subtitle_ass.write_text("[Script Info]\n", encoding="utf-8")
    script_text = task_dir / "script.txt"
    script_text.write_text("鍘熷璇嗗埆鏂囨湰", encoding="utf-8")
    clip_text = task_dir / "clip_text.txt"
    clip_text.write_text("瑁佸壀鏂囨湰", encoding="utf-8")
    forum_post_info = task_dir / "forum_post_info.json"
    forum_post_info.write_text('{"thread_id":"123"}', encoding="utf-8")
    cover_image = task_dir / "璁哄潧灏侀潰鏍囬.png"
    cover_image.write_bytes(b"png")
    logs_dir = task_dir / "logs"
    logs_dir.mkdir(parents=True, exist_ok=True)
    process_log = logs_dir / "funclip_20260326_150000.log"
    process_log.write_text("pipeline ok", encoding="utf-8")
    state_file = task_dir / "state.json"
    state_file.write_text(
        json.dumps(
            {
                "last_completed_step": 9,
                "output_file": str(final_video),
                "step_name": "鏂囦欢鏁寸悊",
            },
            ensure_ascii=False,
        ),
        encoding="utf-8",
    )

    task = UnifiedTask(
        task_id="render-manifest-task",
        task_type=TaskType.VIDEO,
        source="unit",
        source_path=str(tmp_path / "source.mp4"),
    )
    Path(str(task.source_path)).write_bytes(b"source-video")

    result = service._attach_video_render_manifest(
        task,
        {
            "success": True,
            "request_type": "video",
            "engine": "internal_pipeline",
            "output_path": str(final_video),
        },
    )

    artifacts = result.get("artifacts") or []
    roles = {str(item.get("role")): item for item in artifacts}
    assert "final_video" in roles
    assert roles["final_video"].get("is_primary") is True
    assert "subtitle_srt" in roles
    assert "subtitle_ass" in roles
    assert "clip_text" in roles
    assert "forum_post_info" in roles
    assert "cover_image" in roles
    assert "processing_log" in roles
    assert "pipeline_state" in roles

    render_manifest = result.get("render_manifest") or {}
    assert render_manifest.get("schema_version") == "1.0"
    assert render_manifest.get("primary_artifact_id") == roles["final_video"].get("artifact_id")
    subtitles = render_manifest.get("subtitles") or {}
    assert subtitles.get("srt") == roles["subtitle_srt"].get("artifact_id")
    assert subtitles.get("ass") == roles["subtitle_ass"].get("artifact_id")
    texts = render_manifest.get("texts") or {}
    assert texts.get("clip_text") == roles["clip_text"].get("artifact_id")
    assert texts.get("script") == roles["transcript_text"].get("artifact_id")
    context = render_manifest.get("context") or {}
    assert context.get("forum_post_info") == roles["forum_post_info"].get("artifact_id")
    cover = render_manifest.get("cover") or {}
    assert cover.get("image") == roles["cover_image"].get("artifact_id")
    logs = render_manifest.get("logs") or {}
    assert logs.get("processing") == roles["processing_log"].get("artifact_id")
    pipeline_state = render_manifest.get("pipeline_state") or {}
    assert pipeline_state.get("last_completed_step") == 9


def test_internal_pipeline_context_maps_custom_backend_model_to_openai(monkeypatch, tmp_path) -> None:  # type: ignore[no-untyped-def]
    monkeypatch.setenv("CLONECUT_DB_PATH", str(tmp_path / "clonecut_internal_context.db"))
    cfg = _build_config(tmp_path)
    service = WorkerService(cfg)
    task_dir = Path(cfg.output_dir) / "context-task"
    task_dir.mkdir(parents=True, exist_ok=True)
    source = tmp_path / "context-source.mp4"
    source.write_bytes(b"video-content")

    task = UnifiedTask(
        task_id="context-task",
        task_type=TaskType.VIDEO,
        source="unit",
        source_path=str(source),
        payload={"stage5_model_name": "yunyi-codex/gpt-5.4"},
        metadata={"source": "unit"},
    )

    options = service._prepare_internal_pipeline_context(task=task, task_dir=task_dir)

    assert options.get("model") == "openai"
    assert options.get("openai_backend_model") == "yunyi-codex/gpt-5.4"


def test_internal_pipeline_env_forces_utf8_and_backend_override(monkeypatch, tmp_path) -> None:  # type: ignore[no-untyped-def]
    monkeypatch.setenv("CLONECUT_DB_PATH", str(tmp_path / "clonecut_internal_env.db"))
    ffmpeg_bin_dir = tmp_path / "ffmpeg-bin"
    ffmpeg_bin_dir.mkdir(parents=True, exist_ok=True)
    monkeypatch.setenv("CLONECUT_FFMPEG_BIN_DIR", str(ffmpeg_bin_dir))
    cfg = _build_config(tmp_path)
    service = WorkerService(cfg)

    env = service._build_internal_pipeline_env(
        pipeline_inputs={"openai_backend_model": "yunyi-codex/gpt-5.4"}
    )

    assert env.get("PYTHONIOENCODING") == "utf-8"
    assert env.get("PYTHONUTF8") == "1"
    assert env.get("OPENAI_BACKEND_MODEL") == "yunyi-codex/gpt-5.4"
    assert str(Path(sys.executable).resolve().parent) in env.get("PATH", "")
    assert str(ffmpeg_bin_dir.resolve()) in env.get("PATH", "")

def test_tts_task_uses_local_engine_by_default(monkeypatch, tmp_path) -> None:  # type: ignore[no-untyped-def]

def test_build_task_normalizes_forum_post_info_and_source_url(monkeypatch, tmp_path) -> None:  # type: ignore[no-untyped-def]
    monkeypatch.setenv("CLONECUT_DB_PATH", str(tmp_path / "clonecut_forum_normalize.db"))
    cfg = _build_config(tmp_path)
    service = WorkerService(cfg)

    task = service._build_task(
        {
            "task_type": "video",
            "source_url": "https://forum.example.com/thread-123-1-1.html",
            "payload": {
                "video_urls": ["https://cdn.example.com/demo_source.mp4"],
                "hotwords": ["蹇壀", "AI", "ai"],
                "cover_title_up": "涓婃爣棰?,
                "cover_title_down": "涓嬫爣棰?,
                "original_filename": "demo_source.mp4",
            },
            "metadata": {
                "source": "forum",
                "forum_post_info": {
                    "hotwords": ["蹇壀", "璁哄潧"],
                    "灏侀潰鏍囬涓?: "涓爣棰?,
                    "original_filename": "demo_source.mp4",
                },
            },
        }
    )

    assert task.source_url == "https://forum.example.com/thread-123-1-1.html"
    info = task.metadata.get("forum_post_info") or {}
    assert info.get("hotwords") == ["蹇壀", "璁哄潧", "AI"]
    assert info.get("cover_title_up") == "涓婃爣棰?
    assert info.get("cover_title_middle") == "涓爣棰?
    assert info.get("cover_title_down") == "涓嬫爣棰?
    assert info.get("灏侀潰鏍囬涓?) == "涓婃爣棰?
    assert info.get("灏侀潰鏍囬涓?) == "涓爣棰?
    assert info.get("灏侀潰鏍囬涓?) == "涓嬫爣棰?
    assert task.metadata.get("original_filename") == "demo_source.mp4"
    assert task.payload.get("original_filename") == "demo_source.mp4"

def test_run_process_stage_applies_original_filename_naming(monkeypatch, tmp_path) -> None:  # type: ignore[no-untyped-def]
    monkeypatch.setenv("CLONECUT_DB_PATH", str(tmp_path / "clonecut_forum_naming.db"))
    cfg = _build_config(tmp_path)
    service = WorkerService(cfg)

    source = tmp_path / "source.mp4"
    source.write_bytes(b"video")
    task = UnifiedTask(
        task_id="forum-name-1",
        task_type=TaskType.VIDEO,
        source="forum",
        source_path=str(source),
        metadata={
            "source": "forum",
            "original_filename": "forum_final.mp4",
            "forum_post_info": {"original_filename": "forum_final.mp4"},
        },
    )
    service._persist_task(task)

    stage_output = Path(cfg.output_dir) / task.task_id / f"{task.task_id}.mp4"
    stage_output.parent.mkdir(parents=True, exist_ok=True)
    stage_output.write_bytes(b"processed-video")

    def fake_process_video_like(_task):  # type: ignore[no-untyped-def]
        return {
            "success": True,
            "request_type": "video",
            "engine": "internal_pipeline",
            "output_path": str(stage_output),
        }

    enqueued: dict[str, str] = {}

    def fake_enqueue(queue_name, queued_task):  # type: ignore[no-untyped-def]
        enqueued["queue"] = queue_name
        enqueued["task_id"] = queued_task.task_id

    service._process_video_like = fake_process_video_like  # type: ignore[method-assign]
    service._enqueue_task = fake_enqueue  # type: ignore[method-assign]

    service._run_process_stage(task)

    assert enqueued.get("queue") == "upload"
    assert enqueued.get("task_id") == task.task_id
    assert task.output_path is not None
    final_output = Path(task.output_path)
    assert final_output.exists()
    assert final_output.name == "forum_final.mp4"
    assert final_output.read_bytes() == b"processed-video"
    assert stage_output.exists()
    assert task.result is not None
    assert task.result.get("output_path") == str(final_output)
    assert task.result.get("original_output_path") == str(stage_output)
    assert task.result.get("named_output_path") == str(final_output)


def test_apply_video_output_naming_keeps_equivalent_final_output(monkeypatch, tmp_path) -> None:  # type: ignore[no-untyped-def]
    monkeypatch.setenv("CLONECUT_DB_PATH", str(tmp_path / "clonecut_forum_keep_final.db"))
    cfg = _build_config(tmp_path)
    service = WorkerService(cfg)

    final_output = tmp_path / "out" / "璁哄潧鏍锋湰瑙嗛" / "璁哄潧鏍锋湰瑙嗛_final.mp4"
    final_output.parent.mkdir(parents=True, exist_ok=True)
    final_output.write_bytes(b"processed-video")

    task = UnifiedTask(
        task_id="forum-keep-final-1",
        task_type=TaskType.VIDEO,
        source="forum",
        source_path=str(tmp_path / "source.mp4"),
        metadata={
            "source": "forum",
            "original_filename": "璁哄潧鏍锋湰瑙嗛.mp4",
            "forum_post_info": {"original_filename": "璁哄潧鏍锋湰瑙嗛.mp4"},
        },
        payload={"original_filename": "璁哄潧鏍锋湰瑙嗛.mp4"},
    )
    task.source_path and Path(task.source_path).write_bytes(b"video")

    result = service._apply_video_output_naming(
        task,
        {
            "success": True,
            "request_type": "video",
            "engine": "internal_pipeline",
            "output_path": str(final_output),
        },
    )

    assert result.get("output_path") == str(final_output)
    assert result.get("named_output_path") is None
    assert not result.get("original_output_path")
    assert (task.metadata or {}).get("named_output_path") == str(final_output)


def test_upload_output_replies_forum_with_strict_attachment(monkeypatch, tmp_path) -> None:  # type: ignore[no-untyped-def]
    monkeypatch.setenv("CLONECUT_DB_PATH", str(tmp_path / "clonecut_upload_forum.db"))
    monkeypatch.setenv("FORUM_BASE_URL", "https://forum.example.com")
    monkeypatch.setenv("FORUM_USERNAME", "tester")
    monkeypatch.setenv("FORUM_PASSWORD", "secret")
    cfg = _build_config(tmp_path)
    service = WorkerService(cfg)

    output_file = tmp_path / "forum-output.mp4"
    output_file.write_bytes(b"video-bytes")
    task = UnifiedTask(
        task_id="forum-upload-1",
        task_type=TaskType.VIDEO,
        source="forum",
        output_path=str(output_file),
        metadata={"forum_post_info": {"thread_id": "12345"}},
    )

    captured: dict[str, object] = {}

    class FakeReplier:
        def __init__(self, http_client, logger=None) -> None:  # type: ignore[no-untyped-def]
            _ = logger
            captured["base_url"] = http_client.base_url

        def reply_with_attachments(self, thread_id, content, video_files, strict_attachment=False):  # type: ignore[no-untyped-def]
            captured["thread_id"] = thread_id
            captured["content"] = content
            captured["video_files"] = list(video_files)
            captured["strict_attachment"] = bool(strict_attachment)
            return True, ""

    monkeypatch.setattr("apps.worker.service.ForumReplier", FakeReplier)

    upload_result = service._upload_output(task)
    forum_reply = upload_result.get("forum_reply") or {}

    assert upload_result.get("success") is True
    assert upload_result.get("storage") == "local"
    assert forum_reply.get("attempted") is True
    assert forum_reply.get("success") is True
    assert forum_reply.get("thread_id") == "12345"
    assert captured.get("base_url") == "https://forum.example.com"
    assert captured.get("thread_id") == "12345"
    content = str(captured.get("content") or "")
    assert "馃幀 AI鏅鸿兘鍓緫瀹屾垚锛? in content
    assert "馃摑 鍘熷瑙嗛: 鏈煡鏂囦欢" in content
    assert "馃幆 澶勭悊缁撴灉: 1 涓増鏈? in content
    assert "馃摴 forum-output.mp4" in content
    assert "馃晵 澶勭悊鏃堕棿:" in content
    assert "馃 AI鍓緫鍔╂墜 - 鏅鸿兘瑙嗛澶勭悊瀹屾垚" in content
    assert captured.get("strict_attachment") is True


def test_upload_output_replies_forum_prefers_user_report(monkeypatch, tmp_path) -> None:  # type: ignore[no-untyped-def]
    monkeypatch.setenv("CLONECUT_DB_PATH", str(tmp_path / "clonecut_upload_forum_user_report.db"))
    monkeypatch.setenv("FORUM_BASE_URL", "https://forum.example.com")
    monkeypatch.setenv("FORUM_USERNAME", "tester")
    monkeypatch.setenv("FORUM_PASSWORD", "secret")
    cfg = _build_config(tmp_path)
    service = WorkerService(cfg)

    output_file = tmp_path / "forum-output-user-report.mp4"
    output_file.write_bytes(b"video-bytes")
    task = UnifiedTask(
        task_id="forum-upload-user-report-1",
        task_type=TaskType.VIDEO,
        source="forum",
        output_path=str(output_file),
        metadata={
            "forum_post_info": {"thread_id": "12345"},
            "user_report": "杩欐槸鐢ㄦ埛渚ф姤鍛婂唴瀹?,
        },
    )

    captured: dict[str, object] = {}

    class FakeReplier:
        def __init__(self, http_client, logger=None) -> None:  # type: ignore[no-untyped-def]
            _ = http_client
            _ = logger

        def reply_with_attachments(self, thread_id, content, video_files, strict_attachment=False):  # type: ignore[no-untyped-def]
            captured["thread_id"] = thread_id
            captured["content"] = content
            captured["video_files"] = list(video_files)
            captured["strict_attachment"] = bool(strict_attachment)
            return True, ""

    monkeypatch.setattr("apps.worker.service.ForumReplier", FakeReplier)

    upload_result = service._upload_output(task)
    forum_reply = upload_result.get("forum_reply") or {}

    assert upload_result.get("success") is True
    assert forum_reply.get("attempted") is True
    assert forum_reply.get("success") is True
    assert forum_reply.get("thread_id") == "12345"
    assert captured.get("thread_id") == "12345"
    assert captured.get("content") == "杩欐槸鐢ㄦ埛渚ф姤鍛婂唴瀹?
    assert captured.get("strict_attachment") is True


def test_upload_output_forum_4xx_is_non_retryable(monkeypatch, tmp_path) -> None:  # type: ignore[no-untyped-def]
    monkeypatch.setenv("CLONECUT_DB_PATH", str(tmp_path / "clonecut_upload_forum_4xx.db"))
    monkeypatch.setenv("FORUM_BASE_URL", "https://forum.example.com")

        source="forum",
        output_path=str(output_file),
        metadata={"forum_post_info": {"thread_id": "12345"}},
    )

    class FakeReplier:
        def __init__(self, http_client, logger=None) -> None:  # type: ignore[no-untyped-def]
            _ = http_client
            _ = logger

        def reply_with_attachments(self, thread_id, content, video_files, strict_attachment=False):  # type: ignore[no-untyped-def]
            _ = thread_id
            _ = content
            _ = video_files
            _ = strict_attachment
            return False, "attachment upload failed: traditional upload failed: status=403"

    monkeypatch.setattr("apps.worker.service.ForumReplier", FakeReplier)

    with pytest.raises(NonRetryableUploadError):
        service._upload_output(task)


def test_fail_task_skips_retry_for_non_retryable_upload_error(monkeypatch, tmp_path) -> None:  # type: ignore[no-untyped-def]
    monkeypatch.setenv("CLONECUT_DB_PATH", str(tmp_path / "clonecut_upload_non_retryable.db"))
    cfg = _build_config(tmp_path)
    service = WorkerService(cfg)

    task = UnifiedTask(
        task_id="upload-no-retry-1",
        task_type=TaskType.VIDEO,
        source="forum",
        status=TaskStatus.UPLOADING,
        max_retries=2,
    )
    service._persist_task(task)

    service._fail_task(
        task=task,
        error=NonRetryableUploadError("attachment upload failed: status=403"),
        failed_from=TaskStatus.UPLOADING,
    )

    assert task.status == TaskStatus.FAILED
    assert task.retry_count == 0
    assert (task.metadata or {}).get("retryable_failure") is False
    assert "retry_due_at" not in (task.metadata or {})


def test_retry_delay_uses_upload_backoff_series(monkeypatch, tmp_path) -> None:  # type: ignore[no-untyped-def]
    monkeypatch.setenv("CLONECUT_DB_PATH", str(tmp_path / "clonecut_upload_backoff.db"))
    cfg = _build_config(tmp_path)
    cfg.raw["queue"]["retry_backoff_seconds"] = [9, 9, 9]
    service = WorkerService(cfg)

    upload_task = UnifiedTask(
        task_id="upload-backoff-1",
        task_type=TaskType.VIDEO,
        source="unit",
        metadata={"failed_from_status": TaskStatus.UPLOADING.value},
    )
    process_task = UnifiedTask(
        task_id="process-backoff-1",
        task_type=TaskType.VIDEO,
        source="unit",
        metadata={"failed_from_status": TaskStatus.PROCESSING.value},
    )

    assert service._retry_delay_seconds(upload_task, 0) == 1
    assert service._retry_delay_seconds(upload_task, 1) == 2
    assert service._retry_delay_seconds(upload_task, 2) == 4
    assert service._retry_delay_seconds(process_task, 0) == 9


def test_run_download_stage_parses_forum_post_and_writes_forum_info_snapshot(monkeypatch, tmp_path) -> None:  # type: ignore[no-untyped-def]
    monkeypatch.setenv("CLONECUT_DB_PATH", str(tmp_path / "clonecut_forum_parse_download.db"))
    cfg = _build_config(tmp_path)
    service = WorkerService(cfg)

    source_media = tmp_path / "post-source.mp4"
    source_media.write_bytes(b"forum-video")

    task = UnifiedTask(
        task_id="forum-parse-download-1",
        task_type=TaskType.VIDEO,
        source="forum",
        source_url="https://forum.example.com/thread-9876-1-1.html",
        status=TaskStatus.PENDING,
        metadata={"source": "forum"},
        payload={},
    )
    service._persist_task(task)

    parsed_called: dict[str, str] = {}

    def fake_parse(post_url):  # type: ignore[no-untyped-def]
        parsed_called["post_url"] = post_url
        return {
            "post_url": post_url,
            "thread_id": "9876",
            "post_id": "9876",
            "video_url": str(source_media),
            "video_urls": [str(source_media)],
            "original_filename": "forum_topic.mp4",
            "title": "forum title",
            "author_name": "alice",
        }

    queued: dict[str, str] = {}

    def fake_enqueue(queue_name, queued_task):  # type: ignore[no-untyped-def]
        queued["queue"] = queue_name
        queued["task_id"] = queued_task.task_id

    service._resolve_forum_post_download_info = fake_parse  # type: ignore[method-assign]
    service._enqueue_task = fake_enqueue  # type: ignore[method-assign]

    service._run_download_stage(task)

    assert parsed_called.get("post_url") == "https://forum.example.com/thread-9876-1-1.html"
    assert queued.get("queue") == "process"
    assert queued.get("task_id") == task.task_id
    assert task.source_path is not None
    downloaded_path = Path(task.source_path)
    assert downloaded_path.exists()
    assert downloaded_path.name == "forum_topic.mp4"
    assert downloaded_path.read_bytes() == b"forum-video"
    info_path = Path(str((task.metadata or {}).get("forum_post_info_path", "")))
    assert info_path.exists()
    snapshot = info_path.read_text(encoding="utf-8")
    assert '"thread_id": "9876"' in snapshot
    assert '"original_filename": "forum_topic.mp4"' in snapshot

def _build_config(tmp_path, *, runner_mode: str = "subprocess") -> SimpleNamespace:  # type: ignore[no-untyped-def]
    return SimpleNamespace(
        redis_host="127.0.0.1",
        redis_port=6379,
        redis_db=0,
        redis_password="",
        redis_namespace="clonecut_worker_test:",
        input_dir=str(tmp_path / "input"),
        output_dir=str(tmp_path / "output"),
        log_dir=str(tmp_path / "logs"),

                "retry_backoff_seconds": [1],

                "max_download_workers": 1,
                "max_process_workers": 1,
                "max_upload_workers": 1,

                "internal_pipeline_runner": runner_mode,
                "internal_pipeline_pool_size": 1,
                "internal_pipeline_warmup_on_start": False,
                "video_command_template": "",
            },
        },
    )

    return UnifiedTask(

        task_type=TaskType.VIDEO,
        source="unit-test",
        source_path=str(source),

    )


def test_worker_service_start_and_stop_controls_warm_runner(monkeypatch, tmp_path) -> None:  # type: ignore[no-untyped-def]
    monkeypatch.setenv("CLONECUT_DB_PATH", str(tmp_path / "runner_lifecycle.db"))
    events: list[str] = []

    class FakeRunner:
        def __init__(self, **_kwargs) -> None:  # type: ignore[no-untyped-def]
            events.append("runner_init")

        def start(self) -> None:
            events.append("runner_start")

        def stop(self) -> None:
            events.append("runner_stop")

    monkeypatch.setattr(worker_service_module, "InternalPipelineWarmRunner", FakeRunner)

    service = WorkerService(_build_config(tmp_path, runner_mode="warm_process"))
    service.resource_monitor = SimpleNamespace(
        start=lambda: events.append("resource_start"),
        stop=lambda: events.append("resource_stop"),
    )
    monkeypatch.setattr(service, "_recover_stuck_tasks", lambda: 0)
    monkeypatch.setattr(service, "_restore_retry_schedule", lambda: 0)
    monkeypatch.setattr(service, "_spawn_workers", lambda *_args, **_kwargs: None)

    service.start()
    service.stop()

    assert events == [
        "runner_init",
        "runner_start",
        "resource_start",
        "runner_stop",
        "resource_stop",
    ]


def test_run_internal_pipeline_ignores_legacy_warm_runner_and_uses_video_pipeline(monkeypatch, tmp_path) -> None:  # type: ignore[no-untyped-def]
    monkeypatch.setenv("CLONECUT_DB_PATH", str(tmp_path / "video_pipeline_direct.db"))
    service = WorkerService(_build_config(tmp_path))

    source = tmp_path / "source.mp4"
    source.write_bytes(b"video" * 64)
    expected_output = Path(service.config.output_dir) / "video-task-1" / "final.mp4"
    runner_calls: list[str] = []
    captured: dict[str, object] = {}

    class FakeRunner:
        def execute(self, *, payload, timeout_seconds):  # type: ignore[no-untyped-def]
            _ = payload
            _ = timeout_seconds
            runner_calls.append("execute")
            raise AssertionError("legacy warm runner should not be used")

    class FakeVideoPipeline:
        def __init__(self, config, logger=None, performance_tracker=None, resource_monitor=None) -> None:  # type: ignore[no-untyped-def]
            _ = logger
            _ = performance_tracker
            _ = resource_monitor
            captured["output_dir"] = config.output_dir

        def run(self, input_video, task_id, start_from_stage=0, forum_post_info=None):  # type: ignore[no-untyped-def]
            expected_output.parent.mkdir(parents=True, exist_ok=True)
            expected_output.write_bytes(b"done")
            captured["input_video"] = input_video
            captured["task_id"] = task_id
            captured["start_from_stage"] = start_from_stage
            captured["forum_post_info"] = forum_post_info
            return SimpleNamespace(
                success=True,
                output_file=str(expected_output),
                executed_stages=["stage1_transcode", "stage9_organize"],
                performance_summary="video pipeline ok",
                current_stage=11,
                last_stage="stage9_organize",
                failed_stage=None,
                performance_report=None,
            )

    service.internal_pipeline_runner = FakeRunner()
    monkeypatch.setattr(worker_service_module, "VideoPipeline", FakeVideoPipeline)
    monkeypatch.setattr(
        worker_service_module.subprocess,
        "run",
        lambda *args, **kwargs: (_ for _ in ()).throw(AssertionError("subprocess should not run")),
    )

    result = service._run_internal_video_pipeline(_build_task(source), str(source))

    assert runner_calls == []
    assert captured["output_dir"] == str(service.config.output_dir)
    assert captured["input_video"] == str(source)
    assert captured["task_id"] == "video-task-1"
    assert captured["start_from_stage"] == 0
    assert result["output_path"] == str(expected_output)
    assert result["executed_mode"] == "video_pipeline"

    monkeypatch,

) -> None:  # type: ignore[no-untyped-def]
    monkeypatch.setenv("CLONECUT_DB_PATH", str(tmp_path / "video_pipeline_error.db"))

            _ = performance_tracker
            _ = resource_monitor

            _ = forum_post_info
            return SimpleNamespace(
                success=False,
                output_file="",
                error_message="stage6 failed",
                executed_stages=["stage1_transcode"],
                performance_summary="failed",
                current_stage=6,
                last_stage="stage5_ai_text",
                failed_stage="stage6_clip",
                performance_report=None,
            )

    service.internal_pipeline_runner = FailingRunner()
    monkeypatch.setattr(worker_service_module, "VideoPipeline", FailingVideoPipeline)
    monkeypatch.setattr(
        worker_service_module.subprocess,
        "run",
        lambda *args, **kwargs: (_ for _ in ()).throw(AssertionError("subprocess fallback should not run")),
    )

    try:
        service._run_internal_video_pipeline(_build_task(source), str(source))
    except RuntimeError as exc:
        assert "stage6 failed" in str(exc)
    else:
        raise AssertionError("expected video pipeline failure")

def test_stage4_prefers_sidecar_subtitle(monkeypatch, tmp_path) -> None:  # type: ignore[no-untyped-def]
    monkeypatch.setenv("CLONECUT_ASR_BACKEND", "sidecar")
    source = tmp_path / "input.mp4"
    source.write_bytes(b"fake-video")
    sidecar = tmp_path / "input.srt"
    sidecar.write_text(
        "\n".join(
            [
                "1",
                "00:00:00,000 --> 00:00:01,500",
                "hello world",
                "",
                "2",
                "00:00:01,500 --> 00:00:03,000",
                "second line",
                "",
            ]
        ),
        encoding="utf-8",
    )

    out_dir = tmp_path / "out"
    result = stage4_asr.run(input_video=str(source), output_dir=str(out_dir), task_id="v1")
    assert result.success
    assert result.output_file
    assert Path(str(result.output_file)).exists()

    srt = out_dir / "v1" / "_stages" / "v1_stage4_asr_subtitles.srt"

    manifest = out_dir / "v1" / "_stages" / "v1_stage4_asr_manifest.json"
    assert srt.exists()
    assert transcript.exists()
    assert manifest.exists()
    assert "hello world" in srt.read_text(encoding="utf-8")
    payload = json.loads(manifest.read_text(encoding="utf-8"))
    assert payload.get("engine") == "sidecar_srt"
    assert payload.get("fallback_used") is False
    attempts = payload.get("attempts") or []
    assert attempts and attempts[0].get("backend") == "sidecar"

                "validate every stage with tests",
                "",
            ]
        ),
        encoding="utf-8",
    )

    result = stage5_ai_text.run(input_video=str(source), output_dir=str(out_dir), task_id="v2")
    assert result.success
    assert result.output_file
    assert Path(str(result.output_file)).exists()

    script = stage_dir / "v2_stage5_ai_script.txt"
    manifest = stage_dir / "v2_stage5_ai_manifest.json"
    pointer = stage_dir / "v2_stage5_script_path.txt"
    task_clip_text = out_dir / "v2" / "clip_text.txt"
    assert script.exists()
    assert manifest.exists()
    assert pointer.exists()
    assert task_clip_text.exists()
    assert "Script Draft" in task_clip_text.read_text(encoding="utf-8")

    content = script.read_text(encoding="utf-8")
    assert "Script Draft" in content
    assert "Key Points:" in content
    payload = json.loads(manifest.read_text(encoding="utf-8"))
    assert payload.get("engine") == "rule_based"
    assert payload.get("fallback_used") is False
    assert payload.get("strict_rejected") is False


def test_stage5_merges_forum_keywords_when_enabled(monkeypatch, tmp_path) -> None:  # type: ignore[no-untyped-def]
    monkeypatch.delenv("OPENAI_API_KEY", raising=False)
    monkeypatch.delenv("CLONECUT_STAGE5_LLM_MODEL", raising=False)
    monkeypatch.setenv("CLONECUT_STAGE5_USE_FORUM_KEYWORDS", "true")

    source = tmp_path / "input.mp4"
    source.write_bytes(b"fake-video")
    out_dir = tmp_path / "out"
    stage_dir = out_dir / "v5_forum_on" / "_stages"
    stage_dir.mkdir(parents=True, exist_ok=True)
    srt = stage_dir / "v5_forum_on_stage4_asr_subtitles.srt"
    srt.write_text(
        "\n".join(
            [
                "1",
                "00:00:00,000 --> 00:00:02,000",
                "generic transcript sentence",
                "",
            ]
        ),
        encoding="utf-8",
    )

    result = stage5_ai_text.run(
        input_video=str(source),
        output_dir=str(out_dir),
        task_id="v5_forum_on",
        forum_post_info={"hotwords": ["璁哄潧璇岮", "璁哄潧璇岯", "璁哄潧璇岮"]},
    )
    assert result.success
    manifest = stage_dir / "v5_forum_on_stage5_ai_manifest.json"
    payload = json.loads(manifest.read_text(encoding="utf-8"))
    assert payload.get("use_forum_keywords") is True
    assert payload.get("forum_keyword_count") == 2
    assert payload.get("keywords")[:2] == ["璁哄潧璇岮", "璁哄潧璇岯"]

    monkeypatch.delenv("OPENAI_API_KEY", raising=False)
    monkeypatch.delenv("CLONECUT_STAGE5_LLM_MODEL", raising=False)

            ]
        ),
        encoding="utf-8",
    )

def test_stage5_factory_failure_falls_back_to_rule(monkeypatch, tmp_path) -> None:  # type: ignore[no-untyped-def]
    monkeypatch.setenv("CLONECUT_STAGE5_LLM_USE_FACTORY", "true")
    monkeypatch.setenv("CLONECUT_STAGE5_LLM_PROVIDER", "openai")
    monkeypatch.setenv("CLONECUT_STAGE5_LLM_MODEL", "gpt-test")
    monkeypatch.delenv("CLONECUT_STAGE5_LLM_API_KEY", raising=False)
    monkeypatch.delenv("CLONECUT_LLM_API_KEY", raising=False)
    monkeypatch.delenv("OPENAI_API_KEY", raising=False)

    source = tmp_path / "input.mp4"
    source.write_bytes(b"fake-video")
    out_dir = tmp_path / "out"
    stage_dir = out_dir / "v5_factory_fallback" / "_stages"
    stage_dir.mkdir(parents=True, exist_ok=True)
    srt = stage_dir / "v5_factory_fallback_stage4_asr_subtitles.srt"
    srt.write_text(
        "\n".join(
            [
                "1",
                "00:00:00,000 --> 00:00:02,000",
                "factory fallback test",
                "",
            ]
        ),
        encoding="utf-8",
    )

    result = stage5_ai_text.run(input_video=str(source), output_dir=str(out_dir), task_id="v5_factory_fallback")

    manifest = stage_dir / "v5_factory_fallback_stage5_ai_manifest.json"
    payload = json.loads(manifest.read_text(encoding="utf-8"))
    assert payload.get("engine") == "rule_based"
    assert payload.get("llm_use_factory") is True
    assert "api_key" in str(payload.get("llm_error", ""))
    assert payload.get("fallback_used") is True
    assert payload.get("strict_rejected") is False

    def _resolve_forum_base_url(self, post_url: str) -> str:
        configured = str(self._resolve_forum_upload_config().get("base_url", "")).strip()
        if configured:
            return configured
        parsed = urlparse(str(post_url or "").strip())
        if parsed.scheme and parsed.netloc:
            return f"{parsed.scheme}://{parsed.netloc}"
        raise RuntimeError(f"unable to resolve forum base url from post_url: {post_url}")

    def _write_forum_post_info_snapshot(self, task: UnifiedTask) -> None:
        metadata = dict(task.metadata or {})
        payload = dict(task.payload or {})
        forum_info = metadata.get("forum_post_info")
        if not isinstance(forum_info, dict) or not forum_info:
            return

        original_filename = self._resolve_original_filename(
            forum_post_info=forum_info,
            payload=payload,
            metadata=metadata,
            source_url=str(task.source_url or ""),
        )
        if not original_filename:
            return
        normalized_name = Path(self._sanitize_filename(original_filename))
        folder_name = normalized_name.stem if normalized_name.suffix else normalized_name.name
        folder_name = self._sanitize_filename(folder_name)
        if not folder_name:
            return

        output_dir = Path(self.config.output_dir) / folder_name
        output_dir.mkdir(parents=True, exist_ok=True)
        snapshot_path = output_dir / "forum_post_info.json"
        snapshot_payload = dict(forum_info)
        snapshot_payload["original_filename"] = original_filename
        if str(task.source_url or "").strip():
            snapshot_payload.setdefault("video_url", str(task.source_url or "").strip())
        snapshot_path.write_text(
            json.dumps(snapshot_payload, ensure_ascii=False, indent=2),
            encoding="utf-8",
        )
        metadata["forum_post_info_path"] = str(snapshot_path)
        metadata["forum_post_info"] = snapshot_payload
        payload["forum_post_info"] = snapshot_payload
        task.metadata = metadata
        task.payload = payload

    def _guess_download_filename(self, source_url: str) -> str:
        parsed = urlparse(source_url)
        raw_name = Path(unquote(parsed.path or "")).name
        if not raw_name.strip():
            return "source.mp4"
        if "." not in raw_name:
            return f"{raw_name}.mp4"
        return raw_name

    def _parse_file_uri(self, source_url: str) -> Path:
        parsed = urlparse(source_url)
        path = unquote(parsed.path or "")
        if path.startswith("/") and len(path) >= 3 and path[2] == ":":
            path = path[1:]
        return Path(path)

    def _looks_like_windows_path(self, value: str) -> bool:
        if len(value) < 3:
            return False
        return value[1] == ":" and value[0].isalpha() and value[2] in {"/", "\\"}

    def _upload_output(self, task: UnifiedTask) -> Dict[str, Any]:
        output_path = str(task.output_path or "").strip()
        if not output_path:
            raise ValueError("missing output_path for upload")
        source = Path(output_path)
        if not source.exists():
            raise FileNotFoundError(f"output file not found: {source}")
        local_result = self.storage_adapter.upload(task_id=task.task_id, source_path=str(source))
        upload_result = dict(local_result)
        upload_result["forum_reply"] = self._upload_forum_reply_if_needed(task=task, source=source)
        return upload_result

    def _upload_forum_reply_if_needed(self, task: UnifiedTask, source: Path) -> Dict[str, Any]:
        if task.task_type != TaskType.VIDEO:
            return {"attempted": False, "success": False, "reason": "non_video_task"}
        if not self.forum_upload_enabled:
            return {"attempted": False, "success": False, "reason": "forum_upload_disabled"}

        thread_id, has_forum_target = self._resolve_upload_thread_id(task)
        if not has_forum_target:
            return {"attempted": False, "success": False, "reason": "no_forum_thread"}
        if not thread_id:
            raise NonRetryableUploadError("forum thread_id is missing and cannot be parsed from post_url")

        forum_cfg = self._resolve_forum_upload_config()
        base_url = forum_cfg.get("base_url", "")
        username = forum_cfg.get("username", "")
        password = forum_cfg.get("password", "")
        if not base_url or not username or not password:
            raise NonRetryableUploadError(
                "forum upload config missing: FORUM_BASE_URL/FORUM_USERNAME/FORUM_PASSWORD"
            )

        client = ForumHttpClient(
            base_url=base_url,
            username=username,
            password=password,
            logger=self.logger,
        )
        replier = ForumReplier(http_client=client, logger=self.logger)
        reply_content = self._resolve_forum_reply_content(task=task)
        ok, err = replier.reply_with_attachments(
            thread_id=thread_id,
            content=reply_content,
            video_files=[str(source)],
            strict_attachment=True,
        )
        if not ok:
            message = f"forum reply with attachment failed: {err}"
            if self._is_retryable_forum_error(err):
                raise RetryableUploadError(message)
            raise NonRetryableUploadError(message)
        return {
            "attempted": True,
            "success": True,
            "thread_id": thread_id,
            "strict_attachment": True,
        }

    def _resolve_forum_reply_content(self, task: UnifiedTask) -> str:
        metadata = task.metadata if isinstance(task.metadata, dict) else {}
        payload = task.payload if isinstance(task.payload, dict) else {}
        forum_info: Dict[str, Any] = {}
        if isinstance(payload.get("forum_post_info"), dict):
            forum_info.update(payload.get("forum_post_info") or {})
        if isinstance(metadata.get("forum_post_info"), dict):
            forum_info.update(metadata.get("forum_post_info") or {})

        user_report = self._pick_first_text(
            metadata.get("user_report"),
            payload.get("user_report"),
            forum_info.get("user_report"),
        )
        if user_report:
            return user_report
        return self._build_legacy_forum_reply_content(task=task)

    def _build_legacy_forum_reply_content(self, task: UnifiedTask) -> str:
        try:
            metadata = task.metadata if isinstance(task.metadata, dict) else {}
            payload = task.payload if isinstance(task.payload, dict) else {}
            forum_info: Dict[str, Any] = {}
            if isinstance(payload.get("forum_post_info"), dict):
                forum_info.update(payload.get("forum_post_info") or {})
            if isinstance(metadata.get("forum_post_info"), dict):
                forum_info.update(metadata.get("forum_post_info") or {})

            original_filename = self._resolve_original_filename(
                forum_post_info=forum_info,
                payload=payload,
                metadata=metadata,
                source_url="",
            )
            if not original_filename:
                original_filename = "鏈煡鏂囦欢"

            video_files = self._collect_legacy_reply_video_files(str(task.output_path or ""))
            if video_files:
                file_list = "\n".join([f"  馃摴 {name}" for name in video_files])
                file_info = f"馃搧 澶勭悊瀹屾垚鐨勮棰戞枃浠?({len(video_files)} 涓?:\n{file_list}"
            else:
                file_info = "馃搧 瑙嗛澶勭悊宸插畬鎴?

            process_time = datetime.now().strftime("%Y-%m-%d %H:%M:%S")
            return f"""馃幀 AI鏅鸿兘鍓緫瀹屾垚锛?

馃摑 鍘熷瑙嗛: {original_filename}
馃幆 澶勭悊缁撴灉: {len(video_files)} 涓増鏈?
鈿?澶勭悊鏂瑰紡: AI鏅鸿兘鍓緫 + 鍘绘皵鍙?+ 瀛楀箷鐢熸垚

{file_info}

鉁?澶勭悊鍐呭鍖呮嫭:
- 馃攪 绉婚櫎闈欓煶鐗囨鍜屾皵鍙ｅ０
- 馃帳 璇煶璇嗗埆鍜屽瓧骞曠敓鎴?
- 馃幀 AI鏅鸿兘鍓緫浼樺寲
- 馃摑 娣诲姞鏍囬鍜屽瓧骞?

        except Exception as exc:
            self.logger.error("build legacy forum reply content failed: %s", exc)
            return """馃幀 瑙嗛澶勭悊瀹屾垚锛?

鈿狅笍 澶勭悊缁撴灉璇︽儏鑾峰彇澶辫触锛屼絾瑙嗛宸叉垚鍔熷鐞嗐€?

---
馃 AI鍓緫鍔╂墜"""

    def _collect_legacy_reply_video_files(self, output_path: str) -> List[str]:
        text = str(output_path or "").strip()
        if not text:
            return []
        path = Path(text)
        extensions = {".mp4", ".avi", ".mov", ".mkv"}
        if path.is_dir():
            video_files = [
                item.name
                for item in path.iterdir()
                if item.is_file() and item.suffix.lower() in extensions
            ]
            video_files.sort(
                key=lambda name: (
                    "甯﹀瓧骞? not in name,
                    "鏅鸿兘鍓緫" not in name,
                    name,
                )
            )
            return video_files
        if path.is_file() and path.suffix.lower() in extensions:
            return [path.name]
        return []

    def _resolve_upload_thread_id(self, task: UnifiedTask) -> Tuple[str, bool]:
        metadata = task.metadata if isinstance(task.metadata, dict) else {}
        payload = task.payload if isinstance(task.payload, dict) else {}
        source_tag = self._pick_first_text(task.source, metadata.get("source"), payload.get("source")).lower()
        forum_info: Dict[str, Any] = {}
        if isinstance(metadata.get("forum_post_info"), dict):
            forum_info.update(metadata.get("forum_post_info") or {})
        if isinstance(payload.get("forum_post_info"), dict):
            forum_info.update(payload.get("forum_post_info") or {})

        explicit_thread_id = self._pick_first_text(
            forum_info.get("thread_id"),
            metadata.get("thread_id"),
            payload.get("thread_id"),
        )
        post_url = self._pick_first_text(
            forum_info.get("post_url"),
            payload.get("post_url"),
            metadata.get("post_url"),
            metadata.get("source_url"),
            task.source_url,
        )
        forum_like_post_url = post_url if self._looks_like_forum_post_url(post_url) else ""
        has_forum_target = bool(explicit_thread_id or forum_like_post_url or source_tag == "forum")
        if explicit_thread_id:
            return explicit_thread_id, has_forum_target
        parsed = self._parse_thread_id_from_post_url(forum_like_post_url)
        return parsed, has_forum_target

    def _parse_thread_id_from_post_url(self, post_url: str) -> str:
        text = str(post_url or "").strip()
        if not text:
            return ""
        patterns = [
            r"thread-(\d+)-",
            r"[?&]tid=(\d+)",
            r"/forum\.php\?[^#]*\btid=(\d+)",
        ]
        for pattern in patterns:
            match = re.search(pattern, text, flags=re.IGNORECASE)
            if match:
                return str(match.group(1)).strip()
        return ""

    def _resolve_forum_upload_config(self) -> Dict[str, str]:
        base_url = str(os.getenv("FORUM_BASE_URL", "")).strip()
        username = str(os.getenv("FORUM_USERNAME", "")).strip()
        password = str(os.getenv("FORUM_PASSWORD", "")).strip()
        if base_url and username and password:
            return {"base_url": base_url, "username": username, "password": password}

        loaded = self._load_forum_upload_config_from_file(self.forum_settings_path)
        return {
            "base_url": base_url or loaded.get("base_url", ""),
            "username": username or loaded.get("username", ""),
            "password": password or loaded.get("password", ""),
        }

    def _load_forum_upload_config_from_file(self, path_text: str) -> Dict[str, str]:
        path = Path(str(path_text or "").strip())
        if not path.exists():
            return {}
        try:
            import yaml  # type: ignore
        except Exception:
            return {}

        try:
            payload = yaml.safe_load(path.read_text(encoding="utf-8")) or {}
        except Exception:
            return {}
        if not isinstance(payload, dict):
            return {}
        main_forum = (payload.get("forums") or {}).get("main", {})
        credentials = payload.get("credentials", {})
        if not isinstance(main_forum, dict):
            main_forum = {}
        if not isinstance(credentials, dict):
            credentials = {}
        return {
            "base_url": str(main_forum.get("base_url", "")).strip(),
            "username": str(credentials.get("username", "")).strip(),
            "password": str(credentials.get("password", "")).strip(),
        }

    def _is_retryable_forum_error(self, error_message: str) -> bool:
        text = str(error_message or "").strip().lower()
        if not text:
            return False
        statuses = [int(item) for item in re.findall(r"status\s*=?\s*(\d{3})", text)]
        if any(400 <= status < 500 for status in statuses):
            return False
        if any(status >= 500 for status in statuses):
            return True
        if "login failed" in text or "auth" in text or "permission" in text:
            return False
        transient_markers = (
            "timeout",
            "timed out",
            "connection",
            "network",
            "temporar",
            "exception",
            "status=0",
        )
        return any(marker in text for marker in transient_markers)

    def _process_tts_like(self, task: UnifiedTask) -> Dict[str, Any]:
        if not self.tts_adapter_enabled:
            raise RuntimeError("tts adapter is disabled")
        attempts: List[str] = []
        for engine_name, adapter in self._select_tts_adapters():
            if not adapter.is_ready():
                attempts.append(f"{engine_name}: not ready")
                continue
            try:
                result = adapter.process(task)
            except Exception as exc:
                attempts.append(f"{engine_name}: {exc}")
                continue

            output_path = str(result.get("output_path") or "").strip()
            if not output_path:
                attempts.append(f"{engine_name}: empty output_path")
                continue
            result = dict(result)
            result.setdefault("tts_engine_selected", engine_name)
            task.current_stage = 9
            task.stage_checkpoint = f"tts_{engine_name}_completed"
            return result
        raise RuntimeError("tts processing failed: " + " | ".join(attempts))

    def _is_retryable_forum_error(self, error_message: str) -> bool:
        text = str(error_message or "").strip().lower()
        if not text:

            "timed out",

            "status=0",

    def _process_tts_like(self, task: UnifiedTask) -> Dict[str, Any]:
        if not self.tts_adapter_enabled:
            raise RuntimeError("tts adapter is disabled")
        attempts: List[str] = []
        for engine_name, adapter in self._select_tts_adapters():
            if not adapter.is_ready():
                attempts.append(f"{engine_name}: not ready")
                continue
            try:
                result = adapter.process(task)
            except Exception as exc:
                attempts.append(f"{engine_name}: {exc}")
                continue

            output_path = str(result.get("output_path") or "").strip()
            if not output_path:
                attempts.append(f"{engine_name}: empty output_path")
                continue
            result = dict(result)
            result.setdefault("tts_engine_selected", engine_name)
            task.current_stage = 9
            task.stage_checkpoint = f"tts_{engine_name}_completed"
            return result
        raise RuntimeError("tts processing failed: " + " | ".join(attempts))

    def _select_tts_adapters(self) -> List[Tuple[str, Any]]:
        if self.tts_engine_mode == "http":
            return [("http", self.tts_http_adapter)]
        if self.tts_engine_mode == "auto":
            return [
                ("local", self.tts_local_adapter),
                ("http", self.tts_http_adapter),
            ]
        return [("local", self.tts_local_adapter)]

    def _process_video_like(self, task: UnifiedTask) -> Dict[str, Any]:
        source_path = str(task.source_path or "").strip()
        use_internal = self.internal_pipeline_enabled or not self.video_adapter.is_enabled()
        if use_internal:
            if not source_path or not Path(source_path).exists():
                raise RuntimeError("internal pipeline requires a valid source_path")
            engine = "internal_pipeline"
            if not self.internal_pipeline_enabled:
                engine = "internal_pipeline_auto"
            result = self._run_internal_video_pipeline(task=task, source_path=source_path)
            result["engine"] = engine
            return result

        if self.video_adapter.is_enabled():
            result = self.video_adapter.process(task)
            task.current_stage = 9
            task.stage_checkpoint = "video_command"
            return result

        raise RuntimeError("no video engine configured")

    def _run_internal_video_pipeline(self, task: UnifiedTask, source_path: str) -> Dict[str, Any]:
        task_dir = Path(self.config.output_dir) / task.task_id
        task_dir.mkdir(parents=True, exist_ok=True)
        source = Path(source_path)
        if not source.exists():
            task.stage_checkpoint = "stage0_clean"
            task.current_stage = 0
            raise RuntimeError(f"source file not found: {source}")
        stage_names = [
            "stage0_clean",
            "stage1_transcode",
            "stage2_silence",
            "stage3_repair",
            "stage4_asr",
            "stage5_ai_text",
            "stage6_clip",
            "stage6_5_resub",
            "stage7_correct",
            "stage7_subtitle",
            "stage8_cover",
            "stage9_organize",
        ]
        start_from_stage = 0
        pipeline_inputs = self._prepare_internal_pipeline_context(task=task, task_dir=task_dir)

        if self._should_use_internal_pipeline_migration_fallback(source):
            return self._run_internal_video_pipeline_fallback_copy(
                task=task,
                source=source,
                task_dir=task_dir,
                stage_names=stage_names,
                start_from_stage=start_from_stage,
                reason="migration fallback: tiny input",
            )

        pipeline = VideoPipeline(
            config=VideoPipelineConfig.from_env(output_dir=str(self.config.output_dir)),
            logger=self.logger,
            performance_tracker=self.performance_tracker,
            resource_monitor=self.resource_monitor,
        )
        started = time.perf_counter()
        pipeline_result = pipeline.run(
            input_video=str(source),
            task_id=task.task_id,
            start_from_stage=start_from_stage,
            forum_post_info=dict(task.metadata.get("forum_post_info") or {})
            if isinstance(task.metadata, dict)
            else {},
        )
        elapsed_ms = int(max(0.0, (time.perf_counter() - started) * 1000))

        checkpoint = str(pipeline_result.last_stage or pipeline_result.failed_stage or "").strip()
        if checkpoint:
            task.stage_checkpoint = checkpoint
        task.current_stage = int(getattr(pipeline_result, "current_stage", start_from_stage))

        output_path = str(getattr(pipeline_result, "output_file", "") or "").strip()
        self._write_internal_pipeline_state(
            task_dir=task_dir,
            output_path=output_path,
            stage_name=checkpoint,
            current_stage=task.current_stage,
        )

        if not bool(getattr(pipeline_result, "success", False)):
            error_message = str(getattr(pipeline_result, "error_message", "") or "").strip()
            raise RuntimeError(error_message or "video pipeline failed")

        return {
            "success": True,
            "request_type": task.task_type.value,
            "output_path": output_path,
            "executed_stages": list(getattr(pipeline_result, "executed_stages", []) or []),
            "executed_mode": "video_pipeline",
            "performance_summary": (
                str(getattr(pipeline_result, "performance_summary", "") or "").strip()
                or f"video pipeline executed duration_ms={elapsed_ms}"
            ),
        }

    def _should_use_internal_pipeline_migration_fallback(self, source: Path) -> bool:
        threshold_raw = self._get_worker_cfg("internal_pipeline_migration_fallback_max_bytes", 0)
        try:
            threshold = max(0, int(threshold_raw))
        except Exception:
            threshold = 0
        if threshold <= 0:
            return False
        try:
            return source.stat().st_size <= threshold
        except Exception:
            return False

    def _write_internal_pipeline_state(
        self,
        *,
        task_dir: Path,
        output_path: str,
        stage_name: str,
        current_stage: int,
    ) -> None:
        step_mapping = {
            "stage0_clean": 0,
            "stage1_transcode": 1,
            "stage2_silence": 2,
            "stage3_repair": 3,
            "stage4_asr": 4,
            "stage5_ai_text": 5,
            "stage6_clip": 6,
            "stage6_5_resub": 6,
            "stage7_correct": 7,
            "stage7_subtitle": 7,
            "stage8_cover": 8,
            "stage9_organize": 9,
        }
        payload = {
            "last_completed_step": int(step_mapping.get(stage_name, max(0, current_stage))),
            "last_completed_step_name": stage_name,
            "output_file": output_path,
        }
        state_path = task_dir / "state.json"
        state_path.write_text(
            json.dumps(payload, ensure_ascii=False, indent=2),
            encoding="utf-8",
        )

    def _prepare_internal_pipeline_context(self, task: UnifiedTask, task_dir: Path) -> Dict[str, Any]:
        payload = task.payload if isinstance(task.payload, dict) else {}
        metadata = task.metadata if isinstance(task.metadata, dict) else {}
        options: Dict[str, Any] = {}

        forum_info = self._normalize_forum_post_info(payload=payload, metadata=metadata)
        if isinstance(payload.get("forum_post_info"), dict):
            forum_info.update(payload.get("forum_post_info") or {})
        if isinstance(metadata.get("forum_post_info"), dict):
            forum_info.update(metadata.get("forum_post_info") or {})

        original_filename = self._resolve_original_filename(
            forum_post_info=forum_info,
            payload=payload,
            metadata=metadata,
            source_url=str(task.source_url or ""),
        )
        if original_filename:
            forum_info["original_filename"] = original_filename

        if forum_info:
            forum_post_info_path = task_dir / "forum_post_info.json"
            forum_post_info_path.write_text(
                json.dumps(forum_info, ensure_ascii=False, indent=2),
                encoding="utf-8",
            )
            options["forum_post_info_json"] = str(forum_post_info_path)

            next_metadata = dict(metadata)
            next_payload = dict(payload)
            next_metadata["forum_post_info"] = forum_info
            next_metadata["internal_pipeline_forum_post_info_path"] = str(forum_post_info_path)
            next_payload["forum_post_info"] = forum_info
            task.metadata = next_metadata
            task.payload = next_payload
            metadata = next_metadata
            payload = next_payload

        stage5_model_name = self._pick_first_text(
            payload.get("stage5_model_name"),
            metadata.get("stage5_model_name"),
            payload.get("model_name"),
            metadata.get("model_name"),
        )
        if stage5_model_name:
            normalized_model, backend_model = self._normalize_internal_pipeline_model_name(stage5_model_name)
            options["model"] = normalized_model
            if backend_model:
                options["openai_backend_model"] = backend_model

        explicit_backend_model = self._pick_first_text(
            payload.get("openai_backend_model"),
            metadata.get("openai_backend_model"),
            payload.get("openclaw_backend_model"),
            metadata.get("openclaw_backend_model"),
        )
        if explicit_backend_model:
            options["openai_backend_model"] = explicit_backend_model

        file_encoding = self._pick_first_text(
            payload.get("stage5_file_encoding"),
            metadata.get("stage5_file_encoding"),
            payload.get("file_encoding"),
            metadata.get("file_encoding"),
        )
        if file_encoding:
            options["file_encoding"] = file_encoding

        stage5_use_preprocessor = self._extract_optional_bool(
            payload.get("stage5_use_preprocessor"),
            metadata.get("stage5_use_preprocessor"),
            payload.get("use_preprocessor"),
            metadata.get("use_preprocessor"),
        )
        if stage5_use_preprocessor is not None:
            options["stage5_use_preprocessor"] = stage5_use_preprocessor

        clip_text = self._pick_first_text(
            payload.get("clip_text"),
            metadata.get("clip_text"),
        )
        if clip_text:
            clip_text_path = task_dir / "clip_text.txt"
            clip_text_path.write_text(clip_text, encoding="utf-8")
            options["clip_text_file"] = str(clip_text_path)
        else:
            clip_text_file = self._pick_first_text(
                payload.get("clip_text_file"),
                metadata.get("clip_text_file"),
            )
            if clip_text_file and Path(clip_text_file).exists():
                options["clip_text_file"] = clip_text_file

        return options

    def _normalize_internal_pipeline_model_name(self, model_name: str) -> Tuple[str, Optional[str]]:
        raw_model = str(model_name or "").strip()
        if not raw_model:
            return "", None

        normalized = raw_model.lower()
        supported = {"openai", "qwen", "g4f", "deepseek", "kimi"}
        if normalized in supported:
            return normalized, None

        # Old stage5 only accepts provider ids. Route custom backend model ids
        # through the OpenAI-compatible adapter and pass the real backend via env.
        return "openai", raw_model

    def _collect_internal_pipeline_tool_dirs(self) -> List[str]:
        tool_dirs: List[str] = []

        explicit_dir = str(
            os.getenv("CLONECUT_FFMPEG_BIN_DIR", "") or os.getenv("FFMPEG_BIN_DIR", "")
        ).strip()
        if explicit_dir:
            candidate = Path(explicit_dir).expanduser().resolve()
            if candidate.exists():
                tool_dirs.append(str(candidate))

        base_prefix = str(getattr(sys, "base_prefix", "") or "").strip()
        if base_prefix:
            prefix_path = Path(base_prefix).resolve()
            sibling_ffmpeg_dir = prefix_path.parent / "ffmpeg" / "bin"
            if sibling_ffmpeg_dir.exists():
                tool_dirs.append(str(sibling_ffmpeg_dir))

        deduped: List[str] = []
        seen: set[str] = set()
        for item in tool_dirs:
            normalized = str(item).strip()
            if normalized and normalized not in seen:
                seen.add(normalized)
                deduped.append(normalized)
        return deduped

    def _append_internal_pipeline_args(self, cmd: List[str], pipeline_inputs: Dict[str, Any]) -> None:
        model_name = str(pipeline_inputs.get("model") or "").strip()
        if model_name:
            cmd.extend(["--model", model_name])

        file_encoding = str(pipeline_inputs.get("file_encoding") or "").strip()
        if file_encoding:
            cmd.extend(["--file-encoding", file_encoding])

        if "stage5_use_preprocessor" in pipeline_inputs:
            if bool(pipeline_inputs["stage5_use_preprocessor"]):
                cmd.append("--enable-preprocess")
            else:
                cmd.append("--disable-preprocess")

        clip_text_file = str(pipeline_inputs.get("clip_text_file") or "").strip()
        if clip_text_file:
            cmd.extend(["--clip-text-file", clip_text_file])

        forum_post_info_json = str(pipeline_inputs.get("forum_post_info_json") or "").strip()
        if forum_post_info_json:
            cmd.extend(["--forum-post-info-json", forum_post_info_json])

        # Keep root artifacts for worker resolution instead of letting stage9 delete them.
        cmd.extend(["--organize-delete-original", "false"])

    def _build_internal_pipeline_env(self, pipeline_inputs: Optional[Dict[str, Any]] = None) -> Dict[str, str]:
        env = dict(os.environ)
        path_entries: List[str] = []

        python_scripts_dir = Path(sys.executable).resolve().parent
        if python_scripts_dir.exists():
            path_entries.append(str(python_scripts_dir))

        path_entries.extend(self._collect_internal_pipeline_tool_dirs())

        current_path = str(env.get("PATH", "") or "")
        if current_path:
            path_entries.append(current_path)
        env["PATH"] = os.pathsep.join(path_entries)

        # Keep legacy pipeline subprocess I/O stable on Windows even when old
        # Rich logs emit emoji or non-ASCII text.
        env["PYTHONIOENCODING"] = "utf-8"
        env["PYTHONUTF8"] = "1"

        backend_model = ""
        if isinstance(pipeline_inputs, dict):
            backend_model = str(pipeline_inputs.get("openai_backend_model") or "").strip()
        if backend_model:
            env["OPENAI_BACKEND_MODEL"] = backend_model
        return env

    def _resolve_internal_pipeline_output_path(self, task_dir: Path, source_path: Path) -> Path:
        state_file = task_dir / "state.json"
        if not state_file.exists():
            raise RuntimeError(f"internal pipeline state missing: {state_file}")
        try:
            payload = json.loads(state_file.read_text(encoding="utf-8"))
        except Exception as exc:
            raise RuntimeError(f"parse internal pipeline state failed: {state_file}: {exc}") from exc

        last_completed_step = int(payload.get("last_completed_step", -1))
        if last_completed_step < 9:
            raise RuntimeError(
                f"internal pipeline incomplete: last_completed_step={last_completed_step} state_file={state_file}"
            )
        output_file = str(payload.get("output_file") or "").strip()
        if output_file:
            candidate = Path(output_file)
            if candidate.exists():
                return candidate

        patterns = [
            f"{source_path.stem}*_鏅鸿兘鍓緫甯﹀瓧骞曠増*.mp4",
            "*_鏅鸿兘鍓緫甯﹀瓧骞曠増*.mp4",
            "*.mp4",
        ]
        for pattern in patterns:
            candidates = [
                p for p in task_dir.rglob(pattern)
                if p.is_file() and "_stages" not in p.parts and "debug" not in p.parts
            ]
            if candidates:
                candidates.sort(key=lambda p: p.stat().st_mtime, reverse=True)
                return candidates[0]

        raise RuntimeError(f"internal pipeline produced no video output under: {task_dir}")

    def _run_internal_video_pipeline_fallback_copy(

        source: Path,
        task_dir: Path,

        start_from_stage: int,
        reason: str,

        stage_dir = task_dir / "_stages"
        stage_dir.mkdir(parents=True, exist_ok=True)
        output_path = task_dir / f"{task.task_id}{source.suffix or '.mp4'}"
        shutil.copy2(source, output_path)

        asr_srt = stage_dir / f"{task.task_id}_stage4_asr_subtitles.srt"
        asr_srt.write_text(
            "\n".join(

    def _build_internal_pipeline_env(self, pipeline_inputs: Optional[Dict[str, Any]] = None) -> Dict[str, str]:

        path_entries: List[str] = []

        python_scripts_dir = Path(sys.executable).resolve().parent
        if python_scripts_dir.exists():
            path_entries.append(str(python_scripts_dir))

        path_entries.extend(self._collect_internal_pipeline_tool_dirs())

        current_path = str(env.get("PATH", "") or "")
        if current_path:
            path_entries.append(current_path)
        env["PATH"] = os.pathsep.join(path_entries)

        # Keep legacy pipeline subprocess I/O stable on Windows even when old
        # Rich logs emit emoji or non-ASCII text.
        env["PYTHONIOENCODING"] = "utf-8"
        env["PYTHONUTF8"] = "1"

        backend_model = ""
        if isinstance(pipeline_inputs, dict):
            backend_model = str(pipeline_inputs.get("openai_backend_model") or "").strip()
        if backend_model:
            env["OPENAI_BACKEND_MODEL"] = backend_model
        return env

    def _resolve_internal_pipeline_output_path(self, task_dir: Path, source_path: Path) -> Path:
        state_file = task_dir / "state.json"
        if not state_file.exists():
            raise RuntimeError(f"internal pipeline state missing: {state_file}")
        try:
            payload = json.loads(state_file.read_text(encoding="utf-8"))
        except Exception as exc:
            raise RuntimeError(f"parse internal pipeline state failed: {state_file}: {exc}") from exc

        last_completed_step = int(payload.get("last_completed_step", -1))
        if last_completed_step < 9:
            raise RuntimeError(
                f"internal pipeline incomplete: last_completed_step={last_completed_step} state_file={state_file}"
            )
        output_file = str(payload.get("output_file") or "").strip()
        if output_file:
            candidate = Path(output_file)
            if candidate.exists():
                return candidate

        patterns = [
            f"{source_path.stem}*_鏅鸿兘鍓緫甯﹀瓧骞曠増*.mp4",
            "*_鏅鸿兘鍓緫甯﹀瓧骞曠増*.mp4",
            "*.mp4",
        ]
        for pattern in patterns:
            candidates = [
                p for p in task_dir.rglob(pattern)
                if p.is_file() and "_stages" not in p.parts and "debug" not in p.parts
            ]
            if candidates:
                candidates.sort(key=lambda p: p.stat().st_mtime, reverse=True)
                return candidates[0]

        raise RuntimeError(f"internal pipeline produced no video output under: {task_dir}")

    def _run_internal_video_pipeline_fallback_copy(
        self,
        task: UnifiedTask,
        source: Path,
        task_dir: Path,
        stage_names: List[str],
        start_from_stage: int,
        reason: str,
    ) -> Dict[str, Any]:
        stage_dir = task_dir / "_stages"
        stage_dir.mkdir(parents=True, exist_ok=True)
        output_path = task_dir / f"{task.task_id}{source.suffix or '.mp4'}"
        shutil.copy2(source, output_path)

        asr_srt = stage_dir / f"{task.task_id}_stage4_asr_subtitles.srt"
        asr_srt.write_text(
            "\n".join(
                [
                    "1",
                    "00:00:00,000 --> 00:00:01,000",
                    "internal pipeline fallback subtitle",
                    "",
                ]
            ),
            encoding="utf-8",
        )
        cover_manifest = stage_dir / f"{task.task_id}_stage8_cover_manifest.json"
        cover_manifest.write_text(
            json.dumps(
                {
                    "task_id": task.task_id,
                    "engine": "internal_pipeline_fallback",
                    "cover_titles": [],
                    "fallback_reason": reason,
                },
                ensure_ascii=False,
                indent=2,
            ),
            encoding="utf-8",
        )

        executed = stage_names[start_from_stage:]
        task.current_stage = len(stage_names) - 1
        task.stage_checkpoint = stage_names[-1]
        return {
            "success": True,
            "request_type": task.task_type.value,
            "output_path": str(output_path),
            "executed_stages": executed,
            "executed_mode": "fallback_copy",
            "performance_summary": (
                f"internal pipeline fallback executed stages={len(executed)} reason={reason}"
            ),
        }

    def _build_task(self, data: Dict[str, Any]) -> UnifiedTask:
        payload = dict(data.get("payload") or {})
        metadata = dict(data.get("metadata") or {})
        source_path = str(
            data.get("source_path")
            or payload.get("source_path")
            or metadata.get("source_path")
            or ""
        ).strip()
        source_url = (
            data.get("url")
            or data.get("source_url")
            or data.get("post_url")
            or metadata.get("post_url")
            or ""
        )

        task_type = parse_task_type(data.get("task_type", metadata.get("task_type", "video")))
        if task_type == TaskType.VIDEO and not source_url and not source_path:
            raise ValueError("missing source url/source path for video task")

        source_url = self._resolve_video_source_url(
            task_type=task_type,
            source_url=str(source_url or "").strip(),
            payload=payload,
            metadata=metadata,
        )

        forum_post_info = self._normalize_forum_post_info(payload=payload, metadata=metadata)
        if forum_post_info:
            metadata["forum_post_info"] = forum_post_info
            payload["forum_post_info"] = forum_post_info

        original_filename = self._resolve_original_filename(
            forum_post_info=forum_post_info,
            payload=payload,
            metadata=metadata,
            source_url=source_url,
        )
        if original_filename:
            metadata["original_filename"] = original_filename
            payload["original_filename"] = original_filename

        task_id = str(data.get("task_id") or uuid.uuid4())
        priority = parse_task_priority(data.get("priority", "normal"))
        max_retries_raw = data.get("max_retries", metadata.get("max_retries", self.max_retries_default))
        try:
            max_retries = max(0, int(max_retries_raw))
        except Exception:
            max_retries = self.max_retries_default
        retry_count_raw = data.get("retry_count", metadata.get("retry_count", 0))
        try:
            retry_count = max(0, int(retry_count_raw))
        except Exception:
            retry_count = 0
        current_stage_raw = data.get("current_stage", metadata.get("current_stage", 0))
        stage_checkpoint_raw = data.get("stage_checkpoint", metadata.get("stage_checkpoint"))
        try:
            current_stage = max(0, int(current_stage_raw))
        except Exception:
            current_stage = 0
        stage_checkpoint = None
        if stage_checkpoint_raw is not None:
            stage_checkpoint = str(stage_checkpoint_raw).strip() or None

        metadata.setdefault("task_type", task_type.value)
        metadata.setdefault("source", metadata.get("source", "monitor_dispatch"))

        task = UnifiedTask(
            task_id=task_id,
            task_type=task_type,
            source=metadata.get("source", "monitor_dispatch"),
            source_url=source_url or None,
            source_path=source_path or None,
            status=TaskStatus.PENDING,
            priority=priority,
            payload=payload,
            metadata=metadata,
            created_at=datetime.now(),
            retry_count=retry_count,
            max_retries=max_retries,
            current_stage=current_stage,
            stage_checkpoint=stage_checkpoint,
        )
        self._sync_task_metadata(task)

        return task

    def _apply_video_output_naming(self, task: UnifiedTask, result: Dict[str, Any]) -> Dict[str, Any]:
        normalized_result = dict(result or {})
        output_path = str(normalized_result.get("output_path") or "").strip()
        if not output_path:
            return normalized_result

        metadata = dict(task.metadata or {})
        original_filename = self._resolve_original_filename(
            forum_post_info=metadata.get("forum_post_info"),
            payload=task.payload,
            metadata=metadata,
            source_url=str(task.source_url or ""),
        )
        if not original_filename:
            return normalized_result
        if self._is_final_output_already_equivalent(
            output_path=output_path,
            original_filename=original_filename,
        ):
            metadata["original_filename"] = original_filename
            metadata["named_output_path"] = output_path
            task.metadata = metadata
            return normalized_result

        try:
            named_output_path = self._resolve_named_output_path(
                output_path=output_path,
                original_filename=original_filename,
            )
        except Exception as exc:
            self.logger.warning(
                "output naming fallback to stage output: task=%s err=%s",
                task.task_id,
                exc,
            )
            return normalized_result

        metadata["original_filename"] = original_filename
        metadata["named_output_path"] = named_output_path
        task.metadata = metadata

        if named_output_path != output_path:
            normalized_result["original_output_path"] = output_path
            normalized_result["named_output_path"] = named_output_path
            normalized_result["output_path"] = named_output_path
        return normalized_result

    def _attach_video_render_manifest(self, task: UnifiedTask, result: Dict[str, Any]) -> Dict[str, Any]:
        normalized_result = dict(result or {})
        artifacts = self._collect_video_artifacts(task=task, result=normalized_result)
        if not artifacts:
            return normalized_result

        render_manifest = self._build_video_render_manifest(
